	izlude.gat,127,103,3	script	道場挑戰-管理員	734,{

	if (getmapusers("guild_vs1.gat")==0 ) set $party_1,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs2.gat")==0 ) set $party_2,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs3.gat")==0 ) set $party_3,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs4.gat")==0 ) set $party_4,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs5.gat")==0 ) set $party_5,0;

	if (getcharid(1) == 0) goto noparty;
	
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_1) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_2) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_3) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_4) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_5) goto h_party;
	
	goto talk;

noparty:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "您沒有隊伍";
	mes "無法參賽";
	close;
		OnInit:
		waitingroom "道場找我＊",0;
		end;

h_party:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "您是" + getpartyname(getcharid(1)) + "的隊員吧";
	mes "集齊18個xx之心~可在100層打到真金頭盔";
	mes "10層是普通裝";
	mes "20~40層是xx之心";
	mes "50層是王寵封印卡";
	mes "60層是王卡";
	mes "70層是all+3000裝";
	mes "80層是真神";
	mes "90層是背包~機率很低~";
	mes "100層是真金";
	mes "隊伍有報名挑戰, 你要參與嗎？";
	next;
	menu "好的",-,"不用",EXIT;

		if (getcharid(1) == $party_1) goto h_partyin_1;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_2) goto h_partyin_2;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_3) goto h_partyin_3;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_4) goto h_partyin_4;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_5) goto h_partyin_5;

		mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
		mes "你的隊友可能在你報名的時候挑戰結束了！";
		close;
		end;
	
		h_partyin_1:
			if($partywait_1==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs1.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_2:
			if($partywait_2==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs2.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_3:
			if($partywait_3==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs3.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_4:
			if($partywait_4==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs4.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_5:
			if($partywait_5==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs5.gat",49,47;
			end;

		Gone:
			mes "[道場管理-管理員]";
			mes "你的隊友已經先開始了";
			mes "請你等待或換個隊伍另外挑戰！";
			close;
			end;

	EXIT:
		next;
		mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
		mes "隊伍要有3人以上";
		close;
		end;

talk:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "您和您的隊伍想參加嗎？";
	mes "須先繳納10萬元的報名費";
	mes "集齊18個xx之心~可在100層打到真金頭色";
	mes "10層是普通裝";
	mes "20~40層是xx之心";
	mes "50層是王寵封印卡";
	mes "60層是王卡";
	mes "70層是all+3000裝";
	mes "80層是真神";
	mes "90層是背包~機率很低~";
	mes "100層是真金 ";
	next;
	menu "想參加",-,"不用了",EXIT;
	if (zeny<100000) goto nozeny;
	set zeny,zeny-100000;
	StartRand:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs1.gat")!=0 ) goto check1;
	goto check6;
	check1:
		if (getmapusers("guild_vs2.gat")!=0 ) goto check2;
		goto check6;
		check2:
			if (getmapusers("guild_vs3.gat")!=0 ) goto check3;
			goto check6;
			check3:
				if (getmapusers("guild_vs4.gat")!=0 ) goto full;
                       
		check6:
			set @gowhere,rand(6);
			if (@gowhere==0) goto vs1;
			if (@gowhere==1) goto vs2;
			if (@gowhere==2) goto vs3;
			if (@gowhere==3) goto vs4;
			if (@gowhere==4) goto vs5;
	full:
	set zeny,zeny+100000;
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
        mes "[場地一]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_1) + "]";
        mes "[場地二]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_2) + "]";
        mes "[場地三]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_3) + "]";
        mes "[場地四]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_4) + "]";
        mes "[場地五]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_5) + "]";
	mes "全部場地都有人在挑戰了,請稍後再試";
	close;
	end;

nozeny:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "請先湊夠10萬元再來報名";
	close;
	end;

vs1:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs1.gat")!=0 ) goto StartRand;
	killmonster "guild_vs1.gat","vs1_mob";
	warp "guild_vs1.gat",49,47;
	addtimer 30000,"$wait_1";
	set $partywait_1,1;
	set $stage_1,1;
	set $party_1,getcharid(1);
	set $charid_1,getcharid(0);
	enablenpc "裁判#1";
	end;

vs2:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs2.gat")!=0 ) goto StartRand;
	killmonster "guild_vs2.gat","vs2_mob";
	warp "guild_vs2.gat",49,47;
	addtimer 30000,"$wait_2";
	set $partywait_2,1;
	set $stage_2,1;
	set $party_2,getcharid(1);
	set $charid_2,getcharid(0);
	enablenpc "裁判#2";
	end;

vs3:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs3.gat")!=0 ) goto StartRand;
	killmonster "guild_vs3.gat","vs3_mob";
	warp "guild_vs3.gat",49,47;
	addtimer 30000,"$wait_3";
	set $partywait_3,1;
	set $stage_3,1;
	set $party_3,getcharid(1);
	set $charid_3,getcharid(0);
	enablenpc "裁判#3";
	end;

vs4:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs4.gat")!=0 ) goto StartRand;
	killmonster "guild_vs4.gat","vs4_mob";
	warp "guild_vs4.gat",49,47;
	addtimer 30000,"$wait_4";
	set $partywait_4,1;
	set $stage_4,1;
	set $party_4,getcharid(1);
	set $charid_4,getcharid(0);
	enablenpc "裁判#4";
	end;

vs5:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs5.gat")!=0 ) goto StartRand;
	killmonster "guild_vs5.gat","vs5_mob";
	warp "guild_vs5.gat",49,47;
	addtimer 30000,"$wait_5";
	set $partywait_5,1;
	set $stage_5,1;
	set $party_5,getcharid(1);
	set $charid_5,getcharid(0);
	enablenpc "裁判#5";
	end;
}

//======================================== 30F ===================================

guild_room.gat,138,371,4	script	道場挑戰-管理員	734,{

	if (getmapusers("guild_vs1.gat")==0 ) set $party_1,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs2.gat")==0 ) set $party_2,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs3.gat")==0 ) set $party_3,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs4.gat")==0 ) set $party_4,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs5.gat")==0 ) set $party_5,0;

	if (getcharid(1) == 0) goto noparty;
	
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_1) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_2) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_3) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_4) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_5) goto h_party;
	
	goto talk;

noparty:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "您沒有隊伍";
	mes "無法參賽";
	close;
        OnInit:
        waitingroom "３０Ｆ",0;
        end;


h_party:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "您是" + getpartyname(getcharid(1)) + "的隊員吧";
	mes "集齊18個xx之心~可在100層打到真金頭盔";
	mes "10層是普通裝";
	mes "20~40層是xx之心";
	mes "50層是王寵封印卡";
	mes "60層是王卡";
	mes "70層是all+3000裝";
	mes "80層是真神";
	mes "90層是背包~機率很低~";
	mes "100層是真金";
	mes "隊伍有報名挑戰, 你要參與嗎？";
	next;
	menu "好的",-,"不用",EXIT;

		if (getcharid(1) == $party_1) goto h_partyin_1;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_2) goto h_partyin_2;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_3) goto h_partyin_3;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_4) goto h_partyin_4;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_5) goto h_partyin_5;

		mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
		mes "你的隊友可能在你報名的時候挑戰結束了！";
		close;
		end;
	
		h_partyin_1:
			if($partywait_1==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs1.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_2:
			if($partywait_2==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs2.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_3:
			if($partywait_3==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs3.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_4:
			if($partywait_4==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs4.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_5:
			if($partywait_5==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs5.gat",49,47;
			end;

		Gone:
			mes "[道場管理-管理員]";
			mes "你的隊友已經先開始了";
			mes "請你等待或換個隊伍另外挑戰！";
			close;
			end;

	EXIT:
		next;
		mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
		mes "歡迎下次再來。";
		close;
		end;

talk:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "您和您的隊伍想參加嗎？";
	mes "須先繳納20萬元的報名費";
	next;
	menu "想參加",-,"不用了",EXIT;
	if (zeny<200000) goto nozeny;
	set zeny,zeny-200000;
	StartRand:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs1.gat")!=0 ) goto check1;
	goto check6;
	check1:
		if (getmapusers("guild_vs2.gat")!=0 ) goto check2;
		goto check6;
		check2:
			if (getmapusers("guild_vs3.gat")!=0 ) goto check3;
			goto check6;
			check3:
				if (getmapusers("guild_vs4.gat")!=0 ) goto check4;
				goto check6;
				check4:
					if (getmapusers("guild_vs5.gat")!=0 ) goto full;
		check6:
			set @gowhere,rand(6);
			if (@gowhere==0) goto vs1;
			if (@gowhere==1) goto vs2;
			if (@gowhere==2) goto vs3;
			if (@gowhere==3) goto vs4;
			if (@gowhere==4) goto vs5;
	full:
	set zeny,zeny+200000;
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
        mes "[場地一]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_1) + "]";
        mes "[場地二]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_2) + "]";
        mes "[場地三]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_3) + "]";
        mes "[場地四]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_4) + "]";
        mes "[場地五]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_5) + "]";
	mes "全部場地都有人在挑戰了,請稍後再試";
	close;
	end;

nozeny:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "請先湊夠40萬元再來報名";
	close;
	end;

vs1:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs1.gat")!=0 ) goto StartRand;
	killmonster "guild_vs1.gat","vs1_mob";
	warp "guild_vs1.gat",49,47;
	addtimer 30000,"$wait_1";

	set $stage_1,31;
	set $party_1,getcharid(1);
	set $charid_1,getcharid(0);

//======================================== 60F ===================================

guild_room.gat,140,287,4	script	道場挑戰-管理員	734,{

	if (getmapusers("guild_vs1.gat")==0 ) set $party_1,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs2.gat")==0 ) set $party_2,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs3.gat")==0 ) set $party_3,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs4.gat")==0 ) set $party_4,0;
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs5.gat")==0 ) set $party_5,0;

	if (getcharid(1) == 0) goto noparty;
	
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_1) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_2) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_3) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_4) goto h_party;
	if (getcharid(1) == $party_5) goto h_party;
	
	goto talk;

noparty:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "您沒有隊伍";
	mes "無法參賽";
	close;
        OnInit:
        waitingroom "６０Ｆ",0;
        end;

h_party:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "您是" + getpartyname(getcharid(1)) + "的隊員吧";
	mes "集齊18個xx之心~可在100層打到真金頭盔";
	mes "10層是普通裝";
	mes "20~40層是xx之心";
	mes "50層是王寵封印卡";
	mes "60層是王卡";
	mes "70層是all+3000裝";
	mes "80層是真神";
	mes "90層是背包~機率很低~";
	mes "100層是真金";
	mes "隊伍有報名挑戰, 你要參與嗎？";
	next;
	menu "好的",-,"不用",EXIT;

		if (getcharid(1) == $party_1) goto h_partyin_1;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_2) goto h_partyin_2;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_3) goto h_partyin_3;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_4) goto h_partyin_4;
		if (getcharid(1) == $party_5) goto h_partyin_5;

		mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
		mes "你的隊友可能在你報名的時候挑戰結束了！";
		close;
		end;
	
		h_partyin_1:
			if($partywait_1==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs1.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_2:
			if($partywait_2==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs2.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_3:
			if($partywait_3==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs3.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_4:
			if($partywait_4==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs4.gat",49,47;
			end;

		h_partyin_5:
			if($partywait_5==0) goto Gone;
			warp "guild_vs5.gat",49,47;
			end;

		Gone:
			mes "[道場管理-管理員]";
			mes "你的隊友已經先開始了";
			mes "請你等待或換個隊伍另外挑戰！";
			close;
			end;

	EXIT:
		next;
		mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
		mes "歡迎下次再來。";
		close;
		end;

talk:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "您和您的隊伍想參加嗎？";
	mes "須先繳納20萬元的報名費";
	next;
	menu "想參加",-,"不用了",EXIT;
	if (zeny<200000) goto nozeny;
	set zeny,zeny-200000;
	StartRand:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs1.gat")!=0 ) goto check1;
	goto check6;
	check1:
		if (getmapusers("guild_vs2.gat")!=0 ) goto check2;
		goto check6;
		check2:
			if (getmapusers("guild_vs3.gat")!=0 ) goto check3;
			goto check6;
			check3:
				if (getmapusers("guild_vs4.gat")!=0 ) goto check4;
				goto check6;
				check4:
					if (getmapusers("guild_vs5.gat")!=0 ) goto full;
		check6:
			set @gowhere,rand(6);
			if (@gowhere==0) goto vs1;
			if (@gowhere==1) goto vs2;
			if (@gowhere==2) goto vs3;
			if (@gowhere==3) goto vs4;
			if (@gowhere==4) goto vs5;
	full:
	set zeny,zeny+200000;
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
        mes "[場地一]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_1) + "]";
        mes "[場地二]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_2) + "]";
        mes "[場地三]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_3) + "]";
        mes "[場地四]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_4) + "]";
        mes "[場地五]使用隊伍名: [" + getpartyname($party_5) + "]";
	mes "全部場地都有人在挑戰了,請稍後再試";
	close;
	end;

nozeny:
	mes "[道場挑戰-管理員]";
	mes "請先湊夠50萬元再來報名";
	close;
	end;

vs1:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs1.gat")!=0 ) goto StartRand;
	killmonster "guild_vs1.gat","vs1_mob";
	warp "guild_vs1.gat",49,47;
	addtimer 30000,"$wait_1";
	set $partywait_1,1;
	set $stage_1,61;
	set $party_1,getcharid(1);
	set $charid_1,getcharid(0);
	enablenpc "裁判#1";
	end;

vs2:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs2.gat")!=0 ) goto StartRand;
	killmonster "guild_vs2.gat","vs2_mob";

	end;

	killmonster "guild_vs3.gat","vs3_mob";

	set $party_3,getcharid(1);
	set $charid_3,getcharid(0);
	enablenpc "裁判#3";
	end;

vs4:
	if (getmapusers("guild_vs4.gat")!=0 ) goto StartRand;
	killmonster "guild_vs4.gat","vs4_mob";
	warp "guild_vs4.gat",49,47;

	announce "恭喜你,挑戰成功！",17;
	announce getpartyname($party_1) + " 隊伍, 第" + $stage_1 + "關挑戰成功！",17;

	if($stage_1 ==9) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==10) goto ENDING;
	if($stage_1 ==15) goto rest;

	if($stage_1 ==25) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==29) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==30) goto ENDING2;
	if($stage_1 ==35) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==39) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==40) goto ENDING3;
	if($stage_1 ==45) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==49) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==50) goto ENDING4;
	if($stage_1 ==55) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==59) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==60) goto ENDING5;
	if($stage_1 ==65) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==69) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==70) goto ENDING6;
	if($stage_1 ==75) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==79) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==80) goto ENDING7;
	if($stage_1 ==85) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==89) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==90) goto ENDING8;
	if($stage_1 ==95) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==99) goto rest;
	if($stage_1 ==100) goto ENDING9;
	set $stage_1,$stage_1 + 1;
	addtimer 5000,"$Pass_1";
	end;
rest:
	enablenpc "裁判#1";
	announce "休息時間！",17;
	set $stage_1,$stage_1 + 1;
	end;

ENDING:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_1";
	end;


ENDING1:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_11";
	end;


ENDING2:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_12";
	end;


ENDING3:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_13";
	end;


ENDING4:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_14";
	end;


ENDING5:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_15";
	end;


ENDING6:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_16";
	end;


ENDING7:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_17";
	end;


ENDING8:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_18";
	end;


ENDING9:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_19";
	end;
}

guild_vs2.gat,50,47,0	script vs2_mob -1,{
	set $MVPmob_2, $MVPmob_2 - 1;
	if( $MVPmob_2 > 0 ) end;
	announce "恭喜你,挑戰成功！",17;
	announce getpartyname($party_2) + " 隊伍, 第" + $stage_2 + "關挑戰成功！",17;
	if($stage_2 ==5) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==9) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==10) goto ENDING;
	if($stage_2 ==15) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==19) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==20) goto ENDING1;
	if($stage_2 ==25) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==29) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==30) goto ENDING2;
	if($stage_2 ==35) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==39) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==40) goto ENDING3;
	if($stage_2 ==45) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==49) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==50) goto ENDING4;
	if($stage_2 ==55) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==59) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==60) goto ENDING5;
	if($stage_2 ==65) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==69) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==70) goto ENDING6;
	if($stage_2 ==75) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==79) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==80) goto ENDING7;
	if($stage_2 ==85) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==89) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==90) goto ENDING8;
	if($stage_2 ==95) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==99) goto rest;
	if($stage_2 ==100) goto ENDING9;
	set $stage_2,$stage_2 + 1;
	addtimer 5000,"$Pass_2";
	end;
rest:
	enablenpc "裁判#2";
	announce "休息時間！",17;
	set $stage_2,$stage_2 + 1;
	end;

ENDING:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_2";
	end;


ENDING1:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_21";
	end;


ENDING2:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_22";
	end;

	end;

	end;

	end;

	if($stage_4 ==9) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==10) goto ENDING;

	if($stage_4 ==25) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==29) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==30) goto ENDING2;

	if($stage_4 ==39) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==40) goto ENDING3;

	if($stage_4 ==49) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==50) goto ENDING4;
	if($stage_4 ==55) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==59) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==60) goto ENDING5;
	if($stage_4 ==65) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==69) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==70) goto ENDING6;
	if($stage_4 ==75) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==79) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==80) goto ENDING7;
	if($stage_4 ==85) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==89) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==90) goto ENDING8;
	if($stage_4 ==95) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==99) goto rest;
	if($stage_4 ==100) goto ENDING9;
	set $stage_4,$stage_4 + 1;
	addtimer 5000,"$Pass_4";
	end;
rest:
	enablenpc "裁判#4";
	announce "休息時間！",17;
	set $stage_4,$stage_4 + 1;
	end;

ENDING:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_4";
	end;

	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_41";
	end;

	end;

	if ($@mvp_6 ==18) monster "job_sage.gat",49,165,"--ja--",1492,1,"vs6_mob";
 	set $MVPmob_6,5;
 	announce "最後一關挑戰開始,請好好加油！",1;
end;

}

job_sage.gat,49,165,0	script vs6_mob -1,{
	set $MVPmob_6, $MVPmob_6 - 1;
	if( $MVPmob_6 > 0 ) end;
	announce "恭喜你,挑戰成功！",17;
	announce getpartyname($party_6) + " 隊伍, 第" + $stage_6 + "關挑戰成功！",17;
	if($stage_6 ==5) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==9) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==10) goto ENDING;
	if($stage_6 ==15) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==19) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==20) goto ENDING1;
	if($stage_6 ==25) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==29) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==30) goto ENDING2;
	if($stage_6 ==35) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==39) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==40) goto ENDING3;
	if($stage_6 ==45) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==49) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==50) goto ENDING4;
	if($stage_6 ==55) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==59) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==60) goto ENDING5;
	if($stage_6 ==65) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==69) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==70) goto ENDING6;
	if($stage_6 ==75) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==79) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==80) goto ENDING7;
	if($stage_6 ==85) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==89) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==90) goto ENDING8;
	if($stage_6 ==95) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==99) goto rest;
	if($stage_6 ==100) goto ENDING9;
	set $stage_6,$stage_6 + 1;
	addtimer 5000,"$Pass_6";
	end;
rest:
	enablenpc "裁判#6";
	announce "休息時間！",17;
	set $stage_6,$stage_6 + 1;
	end;

ENDING:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_6";
	end;


ENDING1:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_61";
	end;


ENDING2:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_62";
	end;


ENDING3:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_63";
	end;


ENDING4:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_64";
	end;


ENDING5:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_65";
	end;


ENDING6:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_66";
	end;


ENDING7:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_67";
	end;


ENDING8:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_68";
	end;


ENDING9:
	addtimer 5000,"$Ending_69";
	end;
}

//============================================裁判=================================
guild_vs1.gat,50,49,4	script	裁判#1	758,{
	mes "[裁判]";
	mes "您準備要開始挑戰了嗎？";
	next;
	menu "是的",-,"還沒",no;
	next;
	if (getcharid(0) != $charid_1) goto ERROR;
	mes "[裁判]";
	mes "挑戰開始！";
	doevent "chal_1";
	set $partywait_1,0;
	deltimer "$wait_1";
	disablenpc "裁判#1";
	close;
	end;

no:
	mes "[裁判]";
	mes "好的, 請盡速開始";
	close;
	end;

ERROR:
	mes "[裁判]";
	mes "你不是報名的人";
	close;
	end;
}

prt_in.gat,290,126,4	script	壁櫥	111,{
mes "[^FF0000"+strcharinfo(0)+"^000000]";
mes "這是一個壁櫥.";
if(select("查看裡面有什麼","只是一個壁櫥.沒什麼奇怪的")==1) {
mes "^FF0000發現了一個擴音器^000000";
getitem 7040,1;
close;
}
else{close;
}
	}

prt_in.gat,291,130,4	script	花瓶	111,{
mes "[^FF0000"+strcharinfo(0)+"^000000]";
mes "裡面似乎有什麼東西.. 但是憑你自己的一雙手是不能打開的";
mes "找個比較硬的東西吧";
switch(select("查看","離開",callfunc("MS_check",7049,"^FF0000砸碎花瓶^000000"))) {
case 1:
	next;
	mes "[^FF0000"+strcharinfo(0)+"^000000]";
	mes "裡面似乎有什麼東西.. 但是憑你自己的一雙手是不能打開的";
	break;

case 3:
	next;
	mes "你用了石頭把花瓶砸碎了.得到了^FF0000小樹枝^000000";
	getitem 7018,1;
	delitem 7049,1;
	break;

case 2:
	break;
}
close;
}

prontera.gat,152,186,4	script	闖入密室	800,{
mes "傳說中有一位姑娘因為錯誤被關進了畫中.";
mes "你可以瞭解這個秘密並且安全逃出這個密室嗎?";
next;
warp "prt_in.gat",291,124;
close;

bye:
		mes "[闖入密室]";
		mes "玩過了不能再玩哦！";
                close;
}

prt_in.gat,280,140,4	script	一幅畫	111,{
mes "[^FF0000"+strcharinfo(0)+"^000000]";
mes "圖畫中有一個威風凜凜的騎士";
mes "騎士身邊有一個美麗的女人";
mes "你需要石頭1個.紙燈籠1個和擴音器1個才能破解這張畫";
switch(select("查看","離開",callfunc("MS_check",2,7040,"^FF0000打破畫中人^000000",7191,7183))) {
case 1:
	next;
	mes "[^FF0000"+strcharinfo(0)+"^000000]";
	mes "圖畫中有一個威風凜凜的騎士";
	mes "騎士身邊有一個美麗的女人";
	mes "你需要^FF00003^000000個物品才能破解這張畫";
	break;

case 3:
	next;
	mes "你打破了這張畫.從畫中出來了一個女人";
	mes "它告訴了你走出這個密道的方法..";
	next;
        if (g==2) goto bye;
        set g,2;
        getitem 8064,1;
	warp "prontera",155,186;
	break;

case 2:
	break;

bye:
		mes "[闖入密室]";
		mes "周翼只能領1次";
                next;
	        warp "prontera",155,186;
                close;
}
close;
}

function	script	MS_check	{
if(getarg(0)==2){
if((countitem(getarg(1))>=1)&&(countitem(getarg(3))>=1)&&(countitem(getarg(4))>=1)){
return getarg(2);
}
	}      
if(countitem(getarg(0))>=1){
return getarg(1);
}
return "";
}
